faction_infulences_count = {
    set_variable = { infulence_synd = 0 }
    set_variable = { infulence_oppo = 0 }
    set_variable = { infulence_jaco = 0 }
    set_variable = { infulence_sore = 0 }
    #CSP
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CCSP_synd }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_synd = 3 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CCSP_oppo }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_oppo = 3 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CCSP_jaco }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_jaco = 3 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CCSP_sore }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_sore = 3 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_synd }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_synd = 2.4 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_oppo }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_oppo = 2.4 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_jaco }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_jaco = 2.4 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_sore }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_sore = 2.4 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DFA_synd }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_synd = 2.4 }

    if = {

    if = {

        add_to_variable = { infulence_synd = 1.8 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DIS_oppo }

    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DIS_jaco }

    }

        limit = { has_country_flag = DIS_sore }

    if = {

    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DSRG_oppo }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_oppo = 1.8 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DSRG_jaco }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_jaco = 1.8 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DSRG_sore }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_sore = 1.8 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_synd }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_synd = 2.4 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_oppo }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_oppo = 2.4 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_jaco }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_jaco = 2.4 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_sore }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_sore = 2.4 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { dominant_faction_synd_trigger = yes }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_synd = 1.2 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { dominant_faction_oppo_trigger = yes }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_oppo = 1.2 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { dominant_faction_jaco_trigger = yes }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_jaco = 1.2 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { dominant_faction_sore_trigger = yes }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_sore = 1.2 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            dominant_faction_synd_trigger = no
            dominant_faction_oppo_trigger = no
            dominant_faction_jaco_trigger = no
            dominant_faction_sore_trigger = no
        }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_synd = 0.3 }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_oppo = 0.3 }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_jaco = 0.3 }
        add_to_variable = { infulence_sore = 0.3 }
    }

    #BGT
    set_temp_variable = { infulence_synd_temp = seat_synd }
    divide_temp_variable = { infulence_synd_temp = 650 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { infulence_synd_temp = 20 }
    add_to_variable = { infulence_synd = infulence_synd_temp }

    set_temp_variable = { infulence_oppo_temp = seat_oppo }
    divide_temp_variable = { infulence_oppo_temp = 650 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { infulence_oppo_temp = 20 }
    add_to_variable = { infulence_oppo = infulence_oppo_temp }
    
    set_temp_variable = { infulence_jaco_temp = seat_jaco }
    divide_temp_variable = { infulence_jaco_temp = 650 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { infulence_jaco_temp = 20 }
    add_to_variable = { infulence_jaco = infulence_jaco_temp }

    set_temp_variable = { infulence_sore_temp = seat_sore }
    divide_temp_variable = { infulence_sore_temp = 650 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { infulence_sore_temp = 20 }
    add_to_variable = { infulence_sore = infulence_sore_temp }

    #class

    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = 0.01 }

    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = pop_peasants_jaco }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = 0.01 }
    add_to_variable = { infulence_jaco = class_pop_temp }

    set_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = pop_peasants }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = 0.3 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = pop_peasants_sore }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = 0.01 }
    add_to_variable = { infulence_sore = class_pop_temp }

    #
    set_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = pop_merchants }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = 0.3 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = pop_merchants_synd }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = 0.01 }
    add_to_variable = { infulence_synd = class_pop_temp }

    set_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = pop_merchants }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = 0.3 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = pop_merchants_oppo }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = 0.01 }
    add_to_variable = { infulence_oppo = class_pop_temp }

    add_to_variable = { infulence_jaco = class_pop_temp }

    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = 0.3 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = pop_scholars_synd }
    multiply_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = 0.01 }
    add_to_variable = { infulence_synd = class_pop_temp }

    set_temp_variable = { class_pop_temp = pop_scholars }

    add_to_variable = { infulence_synd = class_pop_temp }

    set_temp_variable = { military_temp = military_sore }
    multiply_temp_variable = { military_temp = 0.15 }
    add_to_variable = { infulence_sore = military_temp }

    multiply_variable = { infulence_synd = 10 }

    multiply_variable = { infulence_synd = 0.1 }

    multiply_variable = { infulence_oppo = 10 }
    round_variable = infulence_oppo
    multiply_variable = { infulence_oppo = 0.1 }

    multiply_variable = { infulence_jaco = 10 }
    round_variable = infulence_jaco
    multiply_variable = { infulence_jaco = 0.1 }

    multiply_variable = { infulence_sore = 10 }
    round_variable = infulence_sore
    multiply_variable = { infulence_sore = 0.1 }

    ######

    set_variable = { gui_posynd = infulence_synd }

    set_variable = { gui_pooppo = gui_posynd }
    add_to_variable = { gui_pooppo = infulence_oppo }

    set_variable = { gui_pojaco = gui_pooppo }
    add_to_variable = { gui_pojaco = infulence_jaco }

    set_variable = { gui_posore = gui_pojaco }
    add_to_variable = { gui_posore = infulence_sore }
}

csp_position_change = {
    set_variable = { dominant_faction_synd = 0 }
    set_variable = { dominant_faction_oppo = 0 }
    set_variable = { dominant_faction_jaco = 0 }
    set_variable = { dominant_faction_sore = 0 }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CCSP_synd }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_synd = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CCSP_oppo }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_oppo = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CCSP_jaco }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_jaco = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CCSP_sore }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_sore = 1 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_synd }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_synd = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_oppo }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_oppo = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_jaco }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_jaco = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_sore }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_sore = 1 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DFA_synd }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_synd = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DFA_oppo }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_oppo = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DFA_jaco }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_jaco = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DFA_sore }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_sore = 1 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DIS_synd }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_synd = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DIS_oppo }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_oppo = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DIS_jaco }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_jaco = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DIS_sore }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_sore = 1 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DSRG_synd }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_synd = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DSRG_oppo }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_oppo = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DSRG_jaco }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_jaco = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = DSRG_sore }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_sore = 1 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_synd }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_synd = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_oppo }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_oppo = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_jaco }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_jaco = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_sore }
        add_to_variable = { dominant_faction_sore = 1 }
    }

    faction_infulences_count = yes
}

###     席位变化
#		set_temp_variable = { smc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { src = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { occ = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { oac = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { jnc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { jrc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { soc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { syc = 0 }
#		bgt_seat_change = yes
bgt_seat_change = {
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { smc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { seat_synd_mode = smc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = seat_synd_mode_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { src = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { seat_synd_radi = src }
		custom_effect_tooltip = seat_synd_radi_change_tips
	}
    set_variable = { seat_synd = seat_synd_mode }
	add_to_variable = { seat_synd = seat_synd_radi }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { occ = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { seat_oppo_comm = occ }
		custom_effect_tooltip = seat_oppo_comm_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { oac = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { seat_oppo_anar = oac }
		custom_effect_tooltip = seat_oppo_anar_change_tips
	}
    set_variable = { seat_oppo = seat_oppo_comm }
	add_to_variable = { seat_oppo = seat_oppo_anar }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { jnc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { seat_jaco_neos = jnc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = seat_jaco_neos_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { jrc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { seat_jaco_revo = jrc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = seat_jaco_revo_change_tips
	}
    set_variable = { seat_jaco = seat_jaco_neos }
	add_to_variable = { seat_jaco = seat_jaco_revo }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { soc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { seat_sore_oldl = soc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = seat_sore_oldl_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { syc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { seat_sore_yout = syc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = seat_sore_yout_change_tips
	}
    set_variable = { seat_sore = seat_sore_oldl }
	add_to_variable = { seat_sore = seat_sore_yout }

    while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_mode < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_radi < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_comm < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_anar < 0 }
                check_variable = { FRA.seat_jaco_neos < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.seat_jaco_revo < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.seat_sore_oldl < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.seat_sore_yout < 0 }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_mode < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_mode = 7 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_radi = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_comm = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_anar = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_jaco_neos = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_jaco_revo = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_sore_oldl = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_sore_yout = -1 }
		}
	
        if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_radi < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_mode = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_radi = 7 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_comm = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_anar = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_jaco_neos = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_jaco_revo = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_sore_oldl = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_sore_yout = -1 }
		}

        if = {

			add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_mode = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_radi = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_comm = 7 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_anar = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_jaco_neos = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_jaco_revo = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_sore_oldl = -1 }

            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_anar = 7 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_jaco_neos = -1 }

            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_sore_oldl = -1 }

			add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_mode = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_radi = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_comm = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_anar = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_jaco_neos = 7 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_jaco_revo = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_sore_oldl = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_sore_yout = -1 }
		}

        if = {

			add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_mode = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_synd_radi = -1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.seat_oppo_comm = -1 }

###     阶层好感度变化
#		set_temp_variable = { wc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { pc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { mc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { sc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { bc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { ac = 0 }
#		class_pop_satisfactions_change = yes
class_pop_satisfactions_change = {
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { wc = 0 } }	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction_workers = wc }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = pop_satisfaction_workers
			max = 100
			min = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_satisfaction_workers_change
	}
    if = {
        limit = { 
            has_completed_focus = FRA_entertainment_in_the_factory 
            check_variable = { pop_satisfaction_workers < 50 }
        }
        set_variable = { pop_satisfaction_workers = 50 }
    }


    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pc = 0 } }	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction_peasants = pc }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = pop_satisfaction_peasants
			max = 100
			min = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_satisfaction_peasants_change
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { mc = 0 } }	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction_merchants = mc }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = pop_satisfaction_merchants
			max = 100
			min = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_satisfaction_merchants_change
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { sc = 0 } }	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction_scholars = sc }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = pop_satisfaction_scholars
			max = 100
			min = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_satisfaction_scholars_change
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { bc = 0 } }	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction_bureaucrats  = bc }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = pop_satisfaction_bureaucrats 
			max = 100
			min = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_satisfaction_bureaucrats_change
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { ac = 0 } }	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction_army = ac }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = pop_satisfaction_army
			max = 100
			min = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_satisfaction_army_change
	}

    set_variable = { pop_satisfaction = 0 }
    add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction = pop_satisfaction_workers }
    add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction = pop_satisfaction_peasants }
    add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction = pop_satisfaction_merchants }
    add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction = pop_satisfaction_scholars }
    add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction = pop_satisfaction_bureaucrats }
    add_to_variable = { pop_satisfaction = pop_satisfaction_army }
    divide_variable = { pop_satisfaction = 6 }

    politics_pop_impact_count = yes
    economy_period_change_judge = yes
}

#       随机x个阶层满意度改变x
#       set_temp_variable = { rnum = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { rchange = 0 }
#       random_pop_satisfation_change = yes
random_pop_satisfation_change = {
    custom_effect_tooltip = random_pop_satisfation_change_tt
    hidden_effect = {
        set_temp_variable = { wc = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { pc = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { mc = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { sc = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { bc = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { ac = 0 }
        for_loop_effect = {
            start = 1
            end = rnum
            random_list = {
                1 = { 
                    modifier = { 
                        factor = 0 
                        NOT = { check_variable = { wc = 0 } }
                    }
                    set_temp_variable = { wc = rchange } 
                }
                1 = { 
                    modifier = { 
                        factor = 0 
                        NOT = { check_variable = { pc = 0 } }
                    }
                    set_temp_variable = { pc = rchange } 
                }
                1 = { 
                    modifier = { 
                        factor = 0 
                        NOT = { check_variable = { mc = 0 } }
                    }
                    set_temp_variable = { mc = rchange } 
                }
                1 = { 
                    modifier = { 
                        factor = 0 
                        NOT = { check_variable = { sc = 0 } }
                    }
                    set_temp_variable = { sc = rchange } 
                }
                1 = { 
                    modifier = { 
                        factor = 0 
                        NOT = { check_variable = { bc = 0 } }
                    }
                    set_temp_variable = { bc = rchange } 
                }
                1 = { 
                    modifier = { 
                        factor = 0 
                        NOT = { check_variable = { ac = 0 } }
                    }
                    set_temp_variable = { ac = rchange } 
                }
            }
        }
        class_pop_satisfactions_change = yes
    }
}

###     阶层影响力变化
#       set_temp_variable = { pop_wc = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { pop_pc = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { pop_mc = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { pop_sc = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { pop_bc = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { pop_ac = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { pop_aoc = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { pop_anc = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { pop_asc = 0 }
#       class_pop_change = yes
class_pop_change = {
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_wc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_workers = pop_wc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_workers_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_pc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_peasants = pop_pc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_peasants_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_mc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_merchants = pop_mc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_merchants_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_sc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_scholars = pop_sc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_scholars_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_bc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_bureaucrats = pop_bc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_bureaucrats_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_ac = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_army = pop_ac }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_army_change_tips
	}

    while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_workers < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_peasants < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_merchants < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_scholars < 0 }
                check_variable = { FRA.pop_bureaucrats < 0 }
                check_variable = { FRA.pop_army < 0 }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_workers < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers = 0.5 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_peasants = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_merchants = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_scholars = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_bureaucrats = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army = -0.1 }
		}
	
        if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_peasants < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_peasants = 0.5 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_merchants = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_scholars = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_bureaucrats = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army = -0.1 }
		}

        if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_merchants < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_peasants = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_merchants = 0.5 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_scholars = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_bureaucrats = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army = -0.1 }
		}

        if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_scholars < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_peasants = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_merchants = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_scholars = 0.5 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_bureaucrats = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army = -0.1 }
		}

        if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_bureaucrats < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_peasants = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_merchants = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_scholars = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_bureaucrats = 0.5 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army = -0.1 }
		}

        if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_army < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_peasants = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_merchants = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_scholars = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_bureaucrats = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army = 0.5 }
		}
	}

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_aoc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_army_officers = pop_aoc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_army_officers_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_anc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_army_ncos = pop_anc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_army_ncos_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_asc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_army_soldiers = pop_asc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_army_soldiers_change_tips
	}

    while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_army_officers < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_army_ncos < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_army_soldiers < 0 }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_army_officers < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army_officers = 0.2 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army_ncos = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army_soldiers = -0.1 }
		}
	
        if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_army_ncos < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army_officers = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army_ncos = 0.2 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army_soldiers = -0.1 }
		}

        if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_army_soldiers < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army_officers = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army_ncos = -0.1 }
            add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_army_soldiers = 0.2 }
		}
    }
    army_faction_tendency_change = yes

    set_variable = { gui_popw = pop_workers }
    set_variable = { gui_popp = gui_popw }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popp = pop_peasants }
    set_variable = { gui_popm = gui_popp }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popm = pop_merchants }
    set_variable = { gui_pops = gui_popm }
    add_to_variable = { gui_pops = pop_scholars }
    set_variable = { gui_popb = gui_pops }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popb = pop_bureaucrats }
    set_variable = { gui_popa = gui_popb }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popa = pop_army }

    set_variable = { gui_popao = pop_army_officers }
    set_variable = { gui_popan = gui_popao }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popan = pop_army_ncos } 
    set_variable = { gui_popas = gui_popan }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popas = pop_army_soldiers }
    
    faction_infulences_count = yes
    politics_pop_impact_count = yes

    economy_period_change_judge = yes
}

society_period_change_judge = {
    set_variable = { monthly_change_popswc = 0 }
    set_variable = { monthly_change_popspc = 0 }
    set_variable = { monthly_change_popsmc = 0 }
    set_variable = { monthly_change_popssc = 0 }
    set_variable = { monthly_change_popsbc = 0 }
    set_variable = { monthly_change_popsac = 0 }

    #自然衰退
    set_variable = { popswfade = pop_satisfaction_workers }
    multiply_variable = { popswfade = 0.1 }
    round_variable = popswfade
    multiply_variable = { popswfade = -0.1 }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popswc = popswfade }

    set_variable = { popspfade = pop_satisfaction_peasants }
    multiply_variable = { popspfade = 0.1 }
    round_variable = popspfade
    multiply_variable = { popspfade = -0.1 }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popspc = popspfade }

    set_variable = { popsmfade = pop_satisfaction_merchants }
    multiply_variable = { popsmfade = 0.1 }
    round_variable = popsmfade
    multiply_variable = { popsmfade = -0.1 }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popsmc = popsmfade }

    set_variable = { popssfade = pop_satisfaction_scholars }
    multiply_variable = { popssfade = 0.1 }
    round_variable = popssfade
    multiply_variable = { popssfade = -0.1 }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popssc = popssfade }

    set_variable = { popsbfade = pop_satisfaction_bureaucrats }
    multiply_variable = { popsbfade = 0.1 }
    round_variable = popsbfade
    multiply_variable = { popsbfade = -0.1 }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popsbc = popsbfade }

    set_variable = { popsafade = pop_satisfaction_army }
    multiply_variable = { popsafade = 0.1 }
    round_variable = popsafade
    multiply_variable = { popsafade = -0.1 }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popsac = popsafade }

    ###
    if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 5 } 
                check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 4 } 
            }
        }
        set_variable = { popsfdis = 0.3 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 3 } 
                check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 2 } 
            }
        }
        set_variable = { popsfdis = 0.2 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 1 } 
                check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 0 } 
                check_variable = { DIS_attitude = -1 } 
            }
        }
        set_variable = { popsfdis = 0.1 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { DIS_attitude = -2 } 
                check_variable = { DIS_attitude = -3 } 
            }
        }
        set_variable = { popsfdis = 0 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { DIS_attitude = -5 } 
                check_variable = { DIS_attitude = -4 } 
            }
        }
        set_variable = { popsfdis = -0.1 }
    }
    ###
    set_variable = { popsfev = cof_econ_values }
    multiply_variable = { popsfev = 0.1 }
    round_variable = popsfev
    multiply_variable = { popsfev = 0.1 }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popswc = popsfev }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popspc = popsfev }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popsmc = popsfev }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popssc = popsfev }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popsbc = popsfev }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popsac = popsfev }

    set_variable = { popsfeq = econ_equal }
    add_to_variable = { popsfeq = -50 }
    multiply_variable = { popsfeq = 0.2 }
    round_variable = popsfeq
    multiply_variable = { popsfeq = 0.1 }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popswc = popsfeq }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popspc = popsfeq }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popsmc = popsfeq }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popssc = popsfeq }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popsbc = popsfeq }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_popsac = popsfeq }

    ###
    set_variable = { billpopswc = modifier@monthly_change_popsw }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopswc = monthly_change_popswc }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopswc = popsfdis }

    set_variable = { billpopspc = modifier@monthly_change_popsp }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopspc = monthly_change_popspc }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopspc = popsfdis }

    set_variable = { billpopsmc = modifier@monthly_change_popsm }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopsmc = monthly_change_popsmc }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopsmc = popsfdis }

    set_variable = { billpopssc = modifier@monthly_change_popss }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopssc = monthly_change_popssc }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopssc = popsfdis }

    set_variable = { billpopsbc = modifier@monthly_change_popsb }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopsbc = monthly_change_popsbc }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopsbc = popsfdis }

    set_variable = { billpopsac = modifier@monthly_change_popsa }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopsac = monthly_change_popsac }
    subtract_from_variable = { billpopsac = popsfdis }
}



###     阶层倾向变化    #1工人2农民3小资4知识5官僚6军官7士官8士兵
#		set_temp_variable = { pop_target = 0 }    
#		set_temp_variable = { pop_syndc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { pop_oppoc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { pop_jacoc = 0 }
#		set_temp_variable = { pop_sorec = 0 }
#		class_pop_faction_tendency_change = yes
class_pop_faction_tendency_change = {
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { pop_target = 1 } } #workers 
        workers_faction_tendency_change = yes
    }
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { pop_target = 2 } } #peasants
        peasants_faction_tendency_change = yes
    }
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { pop_target = 3 } } #merchants
        merchants_faction_tendency_change = yes
    }
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { pop_target = 4 } } #scholars
        scholars_faction_tendency_change = yes
    }
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { pop_target = 5 } } #bureaucrats 
        bureaucrats_faction_tendency_change = yes
    }

    #army
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { pop_target = 6 } } #officers
        officers_faction_tendency_change = yes
        army_faction_tendency_change = yes
    }
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { pop_target = 7 } } #ncos
        ncos_faction_tendency_change = yes
        army_faction_tendency_change = yes
    }
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { pop_target = 8 } } #soldiers
        soldiers_faction_tendency_change = yes
        army_faction_tendency_change = yes
    }

    set_variable = { gui_popw_synd = pop_workers_synd }
    set_variable = { gui_popw_oppo = gui_popw_synd }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popw_oppo = pop_workers_oppo }
    set_variable = { gui_popw_jaco = gui_popw_oppo }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popw_jaco = pop_workers_jaco }
    set_variable = { gui_popw_sore = gui_popw_jaco }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popw_sore = pop_workers_sore }

    set_variable = { gui_popp_synd = pop_peasants_synd }
    set_variable = { gui_popp_oppo = gui_popp_synd }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popp_oppo = pop_peasants_oppo }
    set_variable = { gui_popp_jaco = gui_popp_oppo }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popp_jaco = pop_peasants_jaco }
    set_variable = { gui_popp_sore = gui_popp_jaco }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popp_sore = pop_peasants_sore }

    set_variable = { gui_popm_synd = pop_merchants_synd }
    set_variable = { gui_popm_oppo = gui_popm_synd }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popm_oppo = pop_merchants_oppo }
    set_variable = { gui_popm_jaco = gui_popm_oppo }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popm_jaco = pop_merchants_jaco }
    set_variable = { gui_popm_sore = gui_popm_jaco }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popm_sore = pop_merchants_sore }
    
    set_variable = { gui_pops_synd = pop_scholars_synd }
    set_variable = { gui_pops_oppo = gui_pops_synd }
    add_to_variable = { gui_pops_oppo = pop_scholars_oppo }
    set_variable = { gui_pops_jaco = gui_pops_oppo }
    add_to_variable = { gui_pops_jaco = pop_scholars_jaco }
    set_variable = { gui_pops_sore = gui_pops_jaco }
    add_to_variable = { gui_pops_sore = pop_scholars_sore }

    set_variable = { gui_popb_synd = pop_bureaucrats_synd }
    set_variable = { gui_popb_oppo = gui_popb_synd }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popb_oppo = pop_bureaucrats_oppo }
    set_variable = { gui_popb_jaco = gui_popb_oppo }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popb_jaco = pop_bureaucrats_jaco }
    set_variable = { gui_popb_sore = gui_popb_jaco }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popb_sore = pop_bureaucrats_sore }

    set_variable = { gui_popa_synd = pop_army_synd }
    set_variable = { gui_popa_oppo = gui_popa_synd }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popa_oppo = pop_army_oppo }
    set_variable = { gui_popa_jaco = gui_popa_oppo }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popa_jaco = pop_army_jaco }
    set_variable = { gui_popa_sore = gui_popa_jaco }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popa_sore = pop_army_sore }



    set_variable = { gui_popao_synd = pop_officers_synd }
    set_variable = { gui_popao_oppo = gui_popao_synd }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popao_oppo = pop_officers_oppo }
    set_variable = { gui_popao_jaco = gui_popao_oppo }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popao_jaco = pop_officers_jaco }
    set_variable = { gui_popao_sore = gui_popao_jaco }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popao_sore = pop_officers_sore }

    set_variable = { gui_popan_synd = pop_ncos_synd }
    set_variable = { gui_popan_oppo = gui_popan_synd }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popan_oppo = pop_ncos_oppo }
    set_variable = { gui_popan_jaco = gui_popan_oppo }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popan_jaco = pop_ncos_jaco }
    set_variable = { gui_popan_sore = gui_popan_jaco }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popan_sore = pop_ncos_sore }

    set_variable = { gui_popas_synd = pop_soldiers_synd }
    set_variable = { gui_popas_oppo = gui_popas_synd }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popas_oppo = pop_soldiers_oppo }
    set_variable = { gui_popas_jaco = gui_popas_oppo }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popas_jaco = pop_soldiers_jaco }
    set_variable = { gui_popas_sore = gui_popas_jaco }
    add_to_variable = { gui_popas_sore = pop_soldiers_sore }

    faction_infulences_count = yes

    politics_pop_impact_count = yes
}

workers_faction_tendency_change = {
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_syndc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_workers_synd = pop_syndc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_synd_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_oppoc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_workers_oppo = pop_oppoc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_oppo_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_jacoc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_workers_jaco = pop_jacoc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_jaco_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_sorec = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_workers_sore = pop_sorec }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_sore_change_tips
	}

    while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_synd < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_oppo < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_jaco < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_sore < 0 }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_synd < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_synd = 0.3 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_oppo = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_jaco = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_sore = -0.1 }
		}
	
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_oppo < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_synd = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_oppo = -0.3 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_jaco = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_sore = -0.1 }
		}
	
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_jaco < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_synd = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_oppo = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_jaco = 0.3 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_sore = -0.1 }
		}
	
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_sore < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_synd = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_oppo = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_jaco = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_workers_sore = 0.3 }
		}
	}
}

			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_oppo = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_jaco = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_sore = -0.1 }
		}
	
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_oppo < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_synd = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_oppo = -0.3 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_jaco = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_sore = -0.1 }
		}
	
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_jaco < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_synd = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_oppo = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_jaco = 0.3 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_sore = -0.1 }
		}
	
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_sore < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_synd = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_oppo = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_jaco = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_officers_sore = 0.3 }
		}
	}
}

ncos_faction_tendency_change = {
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_syndc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_ncos_synd = pop_syndc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_synd_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_oppoc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_ncos_oppo = pop_oppoc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_oppo_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_jacoc = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_ncos_jaco = pop_jacoc }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_jaco_change_tips
	}
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { pop_sorec = 0 } } }
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { pop_ncos_sore = pop_sorec }
		custom_effect_tooltip = pop_sore_change_tips
	}

    while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_synd < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_oppo < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_jaco < 0 }
				check_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_sore < 0 }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_synd < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_synd = 0.3 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_oppo = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_jaco = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_sore = -0.1 }
		}
	
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_oppo < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_synd = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_oppo = -0.3 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_jaco = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_sore = -0.1 }
		}
	
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_jaco < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_synd = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_oppo = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_jaco = 0.3 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_sore = -0.1 }
		}
	
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_sore < 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_synd = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_oppo = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_jaco = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { FRA.pop_ncos_sore = 0.3 }
		}
	}
}

army_faction_tendency_return = {
    set_temp_variable = { officers_tendc = pop_army_officers }
    multiply_temp_variable = { officers_tendc = 0.01 }
    set_temp_variable = { ncos_tendc = pop_army_ncos }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ncos_tendc = 0.01 }
    set_temp_variable = { soldiers_tendc = pop_army_soldiers }
    multiply_temp_variable = { soldiers_tendc = 0.01 }
}

army_faction_tendency_change = {
    #synd
    set_variable = { pop_army_synd = 0 }
    army_faction_tendency_return = yes
    multiply_temp_variable = { officers_tendc = pop_officers_synd }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ncos_tendc = pop_ncos_synd }
    multiply_temp_variable = { soldiers_tendc = pop_soldiers_synd }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_synd = officers_tendc }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_synd = ncos_tendc }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_synd = soldiers_tendc }

    #oppo
    set_variable = { pop_army_oppo = 0 }
    army_faction_tendency_return = yes
    multiply_temp_variable = { officers_tendc = pop_officers_oppo }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ncos_tendc = pop_ncos_oppo }
    multiply_temp_variable = { soldiers_tendc = pop_soldiers_oppo }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_oppo = officers_tendc }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_oppo = ncos_tendc }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_oppo = soldiers_tendc }

    #jaco
    set_variable = { pop_army_jaco = 0 }
    army_faction_tendency_return = yes
    multiply_temp_variable = { officers_tendc = pop_officers_jaco }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ncos_tendc = pop_ncos_jaco }
    multiply_temp_variable = { soldiers_tendc = pop_soldiers_jaco }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_jaco = officers_tendc }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_jaco = ncos_tendc }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_jaco = soldiers_tendc }

    #sore
    set_variable = { pop_army_sore = 0 }
    army_faction_tendency_return = yes
    multiply_temp_variable = { officers_tendc = pop_officers_sore }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ncos_tendc = pop_ncos_sore }
    multiply_temp_variable = { soldiers_tendc = pop_soldiers_sore }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_sore = officers_tendc }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_sore = ncos_tendc }
    add_to_variable = { pop_army_sore = soldiers_tendc }
}

politics_pop_impact_count = {
    set_temp_variable = { popc_st = pop_satisfaction }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_w = pop_workers }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_sw = pop_satisfaction_workers }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_p = pop_peasants }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_sp = pop_satisfaction_peasants }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_m = pop_merchants }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_sm = pop_satisfaction_merchants }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_s = pop_scholars }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_ss = pop_satisfaction_scholars }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_b = pop_bureaucrats }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_sb = pop_satisfaction_bureaucrats }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_a = pop_army }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_sa = pop_satisfaction_army }

    ####总共

    set_temp_variable = { t1 = popc_st }
    multiply_temp_variable = { t1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { t1 = 0.5 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { t1 = -0.3 }
    set_variable = { t1_show = t1 }
    set_variable = { pop_stability_factor = t1 }

    ####工人

    set_temp_variable = { w1 = popc_sw }
    multiply_temp_variable = { w1 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { w1 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { w1 = popc_w }
    multiply_temp_variable = { w1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { w1 = 2 }
    set_variable = { w1_show = w1 }
    set_variable = { pop_production_factory_start_efficiency_factor = w1 }
    #
    set_temp_variable = { w2 = popc_sw }
    multiply_temp_variable = { w2 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { w2 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { w2 = popc_w }
    multiply_temp_variable = { w2 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { w2 = 1 }
    set_variable = { w2_show = w2 }
    set_variable = { pop_production_factory_efficiency_gain_factor = w2 }
    #
    if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { pop_workers > 35 } 
                check_variable = { pop_workers = 35 } 
            }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { w3 = popc_sw }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w3 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { w3 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w3 = popc_w }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w3 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w3 = 1 }
        set_variable = { w3_show = w3 }
    }
    else = { set_temp_variable = { w3 = 0 } }
    set_variable = { pop_industrial_capacity_factory = w3 }

    ####农民

    set_temp_variable = { p1 = popc_sp }
    multiply_temp_variable = { p1 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { p1 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { p1 = popc_p }
    multiply_temp_variable = { p1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { p1 = 2 }
    set_variable = { p1_show = p1 }
    set_variable = { pop_local_resources_factor = p1 }
    #
    set_temp_variable = { p2 = popc_sp }
    multiply_temp_variable = { p2 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { p2 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { p2 = popc_p }
    multiply_temp_variable = { p2 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { p2 = 1.5 }
    set_variable = { p2_show = p2 }
    set_variable = { pop_conscription_factor = p2 }
    #
    if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { pop_peasants > 35 } 
                check_variable = { pop_peasants = 35 } 
            }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { p3 = popc_sp }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p3 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { p3 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p3 = popc_p }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p3 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p3 = -1 }
        set_variable = { p3_show = p3 }
    }
    else = { set_temp_variable = { p3 = 0 } }
    set_variable = { pop_supply_consumption_factor = p3 }

    ####小资产阶级
    
    set_temp_variable = { m1 = popc_sm }
    multiply_temp_variable = { m1 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { m1 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { m1 = popc_m }
    multiply_temp_variable = { m1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { m1 = 2 }
    set_variable = { m1_show = m1 }
    set_variable = { pop_production_speed_industrial_complex_factor = m1 }
    #
    set_temp_variable = { m2 = popc_sm }
    multiply_temp_variable = { m2 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { m2 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { m2 = popc_m }
    multiply_temp_variable = { m2 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { m2 = 2 }
    set_variable = { m2_show = m2 }
    set_variable = { pop_production_speed_infrastructure_factor = m2 }
    #
    if = { 
        limit = {
             OR = {
                check_variable = { pop_merchants > 35 } 
                check_variable = { pop_merchants = 35 } 
            }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { m3 = popc_sm }
        multiply_temp_variable = { m3 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { m3 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { m3 = popc_m }
        multiply_temp_variable = { m3 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { m3 = -1.5 }
        set_variable = { m3_show = m3 }
    }
    else = { set_temp_variable = { m3 = 0 } }
    set_variable = { pop_consumer_goods_factor = m3 }

    ####知识分子

    set_temp_variable = { s1 = popc_ss }
    multiply_temp_variable = { s1 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { s1 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { s1 = popc_s }
    multiply_temp_variable = { s1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { s1 = 2 }
    set_variable = { s1_show = s1 }
    set_variable = { pop_research_speed_factor = s1 }
    #
    set_temp_variable = { s2 = popc_ss }
    multiply_temp_variable = { s2 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { s2 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { s2 = popc_s }
    multiply_temp_variable = { s2 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { s2 = 1.5 }
    set_variable = { s2_show = s2 }
    set_variable = { pop_compliance_gain = s2 }
    #
    if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { pop_scholars > 35 } 
                check_variable = { pop_scholars = 35 } 
            }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { s3 = popc_ss }
        multiply_temp_variable = { s3 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { s3 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { s3 = popc_s }
        multiply_temp_variable = { s3 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { s3 = 1 }
        set_variable = { s3_show = s3 }
    }
    else = { set_temp_variable = { s3 = 0 } }
    set_variable = { pop_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = s3 }

    ####官僚
    
    set_temp_variable = { b1 = popc_sb }
    multiply_temp_variable = { b1 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { b1 = popc_b }
    multiply_temp_variable = { b1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { b1 = 2.5 }
    set_variable = { b1_show = b1 }
    set_variable = { pop_political_power_factor = b1 }
    #
    set_temp_variable = { b2 = popc_sb }
    multiply_temp_variable = { b2 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { b2 = popc_b }
    multiply_temp_variable = { b2 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { b2 = -3 }
    set_variable = { b2_show = b2 }
    set_variable = { pop_political_advisor_cost_factor = b2 }
    #
    if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { pop_bureaucrats > 35 } 
                check_variable = { pop_bureaucrats = 35 } 
            }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { b3 = popc_sb }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b3 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b3 = popc_b }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b3 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b3 = 10 }
        set_variable = { b3_show = b3 }
    }
    else = { set_temp_variable = { b3 = 0 } }
    set_variable = { pop_political_power_gain = b3 }

    ####军队

    set_temp_variable = { popc_ao = pop_army_officers }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_an = pop_army_ncos }
    set_temp_variable = { popc_as = pop_army_soldier }

    ##军官
    set_temp_variable = { ao1 = popc_sa }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ao1 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { ao1 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ao1 = popc_a }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ao1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ao1 = popc_ao }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ao1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { ao1 = 5 }
    set_variable = { ao1_show = ao1 }
    set_variable = { pop_max_planning = ao1 }

    ##士官
    set_temp_variable = { an1 = popc_sa }
    multiply_temp_variable = { an1 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { an1 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { an1 = popc_a }
    multiply_temp_variable = { an1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { an1 = popc_an }
    multiply_temp_variable = { an1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { an1 = 5 }
    set_variable = { an1_show = an1 }
    set_variable = { pop_army_org_factor = an1 }

    ##士兵
    set_temp_variable = { as1 = popc_sa }
    multiply_temp_variable = { as1 = 0.01 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { as1 = -0.5 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { as1 = popc_a }
    multiply_temp_variable = { as1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { as1 = popc_as }
    multiply_temp_variable = { as1 = 0.01 }
    multiply_temp_variable = { as1 = -5 }
    set_variable = { as1_show = as1 }
    set_variable = { pop_org_loss_when_moving = as1 }

    #
    if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { pop_army > 35 } 
                check_variable = { pop_army = 35 } 
            }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { a1 = popc_sa }
        multiply_temp_variable = { a1 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { a1 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { a1 = popc_a }
        multiply_temp_variable = { a1 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { a1 = 2 }
        set_variable = { a1_show = a1 }
    }
    else = { set_temp_variable = { a1 = 0 } }
    set_variable = { pop_army_attack_factor = a1 }

    ###extra
    if = {
        limit = { has_completed_focus = FRA_civilian_science_funding }
        set_temp_variable = { t2 = popc_st }
        multiply_temp_variable = { t2 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { t2 = 0.5 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { t2 = -0.2 }
        set_variable = { t2_show = t2 }
        add_to_variable = { pop_research_speed_factor = t2 }
    }

    #工人
    if = {
        limit = { 
            has_completed_focus = FRA_everything_goes_to_CGT
            has_completed_focus = FRA_new_proletariat 
        }
        set_temp_variable = { w4 = popc_sw }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w4 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { w4 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w4 = popc_w }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w4 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w4 = 1 }
        set_variable = { w4_show = w4 }
        add_to_variable = { pop_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = w4 }

        set_temp_variable = { w5 = popc_sw }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w5 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { w5 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w5 = popc_w }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w5 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { w5 = 1 }
        set_variable = { w5_show = w5 }
        set_variable = { pop_global_building_slots_factor = w5 }
    }
    else = {
        set_variable = { pop_global_building_slots_factor = 0 }
    }

    #农民
    if = {
        limit = { has_completed_focus = FRA_subsidizing_subsistence_farmers }
        set_temp_variable = { p4 = popc_sp }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p4 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { p4 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p4 = popc_p }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p4 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p4 = -1 }
        set_variable = { p4_show = p4 }
        add_to_variable = { pop_supply_consumption_factor = p4 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = {
            has_completed_focus = FRA_unions_are_not_just_for_labor
            has_completed_focus = FRA_new_proletariat 
        }
        set_temp_variable = { p5 = popc_sp }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p5 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { p5 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p5 = popc_p }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p5 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { p5 = -1 }
        set_variable = { p5_show = p5 }
        add_to_variable = { pop_consumer_goods_factor = p5 }
    }

    #小资
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_completed_focus = FRA_unions_are_not_just_for_labor
            has_completed_focus = FRA_new_proletariat 
        }
        set_temp_variable = { m4 = popc_sm }
        multiply_temp_variable = { m4 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { m4 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { m4 = popc_p }
        multiply_temp_variable = { m4 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { m4 = -1 }
        set_variable = { m4_show = m4 }
        add_to_variable = { pop_industrial_capacity_factory = m4 }
    }

    #知青

    #官僚
    if = {
        limit = { has_completed_focus = FRA_central_planning_commission }
        set_temp_variable = { b4 = popc_sb }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b4 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b4 = popc_b }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b4 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b4 = 1 }
        set_variable = { b4_show = b4 }
        add_to_variable = { pop_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = b4 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_completed_focus = FRA_industrial_technocrat }
        set_temp_variable = { b5 = popc_sb }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b5 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { b5 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b5 = popc_b }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b5 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b5 = 1 }
        set_variable = { b5_show = b5 }
        add_to_variable = { pop_industrial_capacity_factory = b5 }

        set_temp_variable = { b6 = popc_sb }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b6 = 0.01 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { b6 = -0.5 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b6 = popc_b }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b6 = 0.01 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { b6 = 1 }
        set_variable = { b6_show = b6 }
        add_to_variable = { pop_production_speed_buildings_factor = b6 }
    }
    #军官

    #士官

    #士兵

    ####
    force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
}

###     权力倾向改变
#       set_temp_variable = { ppvc = 0 }
#       cof_politics_BGT_vs_CSP_values_change = yes
cof_politics_BGT_vs_CSP_values_change = {
    add_to_variable = { Cof_BGT_vs_CSP_value = ppvc }
    custom_effect_tooltip = cof_politics_BGT_vs_CSP_values_change_tips

    if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { Cof_BGT_vs_CSP_value > 0 }
                check_variable = { Cof_BGT_vs_CSP_value = 0 }
            }
        }
        set_variable = { gui_csp = Cof_BGT_vs_CSP_value }
        multiply_variable = { gui_csp = -0.25 }
        add_to_variable = { gui_csp = 25 }
    }
    else = {
        set_variable = { gui_bgt = 25 }
        set_temp_variable = { t = Cof_BGT_vs_CSP_value }
        multiply_temp_variable = { t = -0.25 }
        add_to_variable = { gui_bgt = t }
    }
    
}

cof_politics_BGT_vs_CSP_values_sic_change = {
    if = {
		limit = { 
            OR = {
                check_variable = { Cof_BGT_vs_CSP_value > 90 } 
                check_variable = { Cof_BGT_vs_CSP_value = 90 } 
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = { FRA_comite_de_salut_public = { NOT = { has_trait = FRA_CSP_buff5 } } }

                character = FRA_comite_de_salut_public

                trait = FRA_CSP_buff5

###     斗争烈度变化
intensity_of_struggle_period_change = {
    set_variable = { iosc = 5 }

    set_temp_variable = { t1 = infulence_synd }
    multiply_temp_variable = { t1 = -1 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { t1 = 50 }
    divide_temp_variable = { t1 = 25 }

    set_temp_variable = { t2 = infulence_oppo }
    multiply_temp_variable = { t2 = -1 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { t2 = 50 }
    divide_temp_variable = { t2 = 25 }

    set_temp_variable = { t3 = infulence_jaco }
    multiply_temp_variable = { t3 = -1 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { t3 = 50 }
    divide_temp_variable = { t3 = 25 }

    set_temp_variable = { t4 = infulence_sore }
    multiply_temp_variable = { t4 = -1 }
    add_to_temp_variable = { t4 = 50 }
    divide_temp_variable = { t4 = 25 }

    multiply_variable = { iosc = t1 }
    multiply_variable = { iosc = t2 }
    multiply_variable = { iosc = t3 }
    multiply_variable = { iosc = t4 }

    multiply_variable = { iosc = 0.1 }

    set_variable = { monthly_change_iosc = 0 }
    add_to_variable = { monthly_change_iosc = iosc }

    set_variable = { stabilitycfios = Cof_politics_intensity_of_struggle }
    multiply_variable = { stabilitycfios = 0.01 }
	multiply_variable = { stabilitycfios = -0.05 }

    set_variable = { ppcfios = Cof_politics_intensity_of_struggle }
	multiply_variable = { ppcfios = -0.3 }
}

#       set_temp_variable = { iosc = 0 }
#       intensity_of_struggle_change = yes
intensity_of_struggle_change = {
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { iosc = 0 } } }
    else = {
        add_to_variable = { Cof_politics_intensity_of_struggle = iosc }
        custom_effect_tooltip = intensity_of_struggle_change_tips

        clamp_variable = {
            var = Cof_politics_intensity_of_struggle
            min = 0
            max = 100
        }
    }

    set_variable = { gui_ios = Cof_politics_intensity_of_struggle }
    multiply_variable = { gui_ios = 0.5 }
    add_to_variable = { gui_ios = 50 }
}

###     议案投票
#       set_temp_variable = { vta_smc = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { vta_src = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { vta_occ = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { vta_oac = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { vta_jnc = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { vta_jrc = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { vta_soc = 0 }
#       set_temp_variable = { vta_syc = 0 }
#       Cof_politics_faction_agree_vote_change = yes
Cof_politics_faction_agree_vote_change = {
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_smc = 0 } } }
    else = {
        set_temp_variable = { t = agree_synd_mode }
        add_to_temp_variable = { t = vta_smc }
        if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t > seat_synd_mode } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_smc = t }
			add_to_temp_variable = { vta_smc = seat_synd_mode }
			add_to_variable = { agree_synd_mode = vta_smc }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_smc = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_synd_mode_change }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t < 0 } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_smc = t }
			add_to_variable = { agree_synd_mode = vta_smc }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_smc = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_synd_mode_change }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { agree_synd_mode = vta_smc }
			custom_effect_tooltip = agree_synd_mode_change
		}
    }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_src = 0 } } }
    else = {
        set_temp_variable = { t = agree_synd_radi }
        add_to_temp_variable = { t = vta_src }
        if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t > seat_synd_radi } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_src = t }
			add_to_temp_variable = { vta_src = seat_synd_radi }
			add_to_variable = { agree_synd_radi = vta_src }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_src = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_synd_radi_change }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t < 0 } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_src = t }
			add_to_variable = { agree_synd_radi = vta_src }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_src = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_synd_radi_change }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { agree_synd_radi = vta_src }
			custom_effect_tooltip = agree_synd_radi_change
		}
    }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_occ = 0 } } }
    else = {
        set_temp_variable = { t = agree_oppo_comm }
        add_to_temp_variable = { t = vta_occ }
        if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t > seat_oppo_comm } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_occ = t }
			add_to_temp_variable = { vta_occ = seat_oppo_comm }
			add_to_variable = { agree_oppo_comm = vta_occ }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_occ = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_oppo_comm_change }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t < 0 } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_occ = t }
			add_to_variable = { agree_oppo_comm = vta_occ }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_occ = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_oppo_comm_change }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { agree_oppo_comm = vta_occ }
			custom_effect_tooltip = agree_oppo_comm_change
		}
    }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_oac = 0 } } }
    else = {
        set_temp_variable = { t = agree_oppo_anar }
        add_to_temp_variable = { t = vta_oac }
        if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t > seat_oppo_anar } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_oac = t }
			add_to_temp_variable = { vta_oac = seat_oppo_anar }
			add_to_variable = { agree_oppo_anar = vta_oac }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_oac = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_oppo_anar_change }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t < 0 } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_oac = t }
			add_to_variable = { agree_oppo_anar = vta_oac }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_oac = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_oppo_anar_change }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { agree_oppo_anar = vta_oac }
			custom_effect_tooltip = agree_oppo_anar_change
		}
    }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_jnc = 0 } } }
    else = {
        set_temp_variable = { t = agree_jaco_neos }
        add_to_temp_variable = { t = vta_jnc }
        if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t > seat_jaco_neos } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_jnc = t }
			add_to_temp_variable = { vta_jnc = seat_jaco_neos }
			add_to_variable = { agree_jaco_neos = vta_jnc }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_jnc = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_jaco_neos_change }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t < 0 } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_jnc = t }
			add_to_variable = { agree_jaco_neos = vta_jnc }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_jnc = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_jaco_neos_change }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { agree_jaco_neos = vta_jnc }
			custom_effect_tooltip = agree_jaco_neos_change
		}
    }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_jrc = 0 } } }
    else = {
        set_temp_variable = { t = agree_jaco_revo }
        add_to_temp_variable = { t = vta_jrc }
        if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t > seat_jaco_revo } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_jrc = t }
			add_to_temp_variable = { vta_jrc = seat_jaco_revo }
			add_to_variable = { agree_jaco_revo = vta_jrc }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_jrc = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_jaco_revo_change }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t < 0 } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_jrc = t }
			add_to_variable = { agree_jaco_revo = vta_jrc }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_jrc = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_jaco_revo_change }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { agree_jaco_revo = vta_jrc }
			custom_effect_tooltip = agree_jaco_revo_change
		}
    }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_soc = 0 } } }
    else = {
        set_temp_variable = { t = agree_sore_oldl }
        add_to_temp_variable = { t = vta_soc }
        if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t > seat_sore_oldl } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_soc = t }
			add_to_temp_variable = { vta_soc = seat_sore_oldl }
			add_to_variable = { agree_sore_oldl = vta_soc }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_soc = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_sore_oldl_change }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t < 0 } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_soc = t }
			add_to_variable = { agree_sore_oldl = vta_soc }
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_soc = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_sore_oldl_change }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { agree_sore_oldl = vta_soc }
			custom_effect_tooltip = agree_sore_oldl_change
		}
    }

    if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_syc = 0 } } }
    else = {
        set_temp_variable = { t = agree_sore_yout }
        add_to_temp_variable = { t = vta_syc }
        if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t > seat_sore_yout } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_syc = t }
			add_to_temp_variable = { vta_syc = seat_sore_yout }
			add_to_variable = { agree_sore_yout = vta_syc }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_syc = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_sore_yout_change }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { check_variable = { t < 0 } } 
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { vta_syc = t }
			add_to_variable = { agree_sore_yout = vta_syc }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_syc = 0 } } }
            else = { custom_effect_tooltip = agree_sore_yout_change }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { agree_sore_yout = vta_syc }
			custom_effect_tooltip = agree_sore_yout_change
		}
    }

    Cof_politics_voting_for_bill_agree_count = yes
    refresh_bgt_seat = yes
}

Cof_politics_voting_for_bill_agree_count = {
    set_variable = { agree_vote = 0 }
    add_to_variable = { agree_vote = agree_synd_mode }
    add_to_variable = { agree_vote = agree_synd_radi }
    add_to_variable = { agree_vote = agree_oppo_comm }
    add_to_variable = { agree_vote = agree_oppo_anar }
    add_to_variable = { agree_vote = agree_jaco_neos }
    add_to_variable = { agree_vote = agree_jaco_revo }
    add_to_variable = { agree_vote = agree_sore_oldl }
    add_to_variable = { agree_vote = agree_sore_yout }
}

bill_to_judge = {
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { agree_vote > 326 } }
        custom_effect_tooltip = bill_pass
        hidden_effect = { bill_pass_effect = yes }
    }
    else = { 
        custom_effect_tooltip = bill_not_pass 
        hidden_effect = { bill_not_pass_effect = yes }
    }
    
    clr_country_flag = voting_for_bill

    clr_country_flag = party_CNS_choice
    clr_country_flag = party_PSF_choice
    clr_country_flag = party_POU_choice
    clr_country_flag = party_CSR_choice
    clr_country_flag = party_PCOP_choice
    clr_country_flag = party_AFA_choice
    clr_country_flag = party_LJR_choice
    clr_country_flag = party_FSR_choice
    clr_country_flag = party_FNC_choice
    clr_country_flag = party_FCF_choice
    clr_country_flag = party_FP_choice
    clr_country_flag = party_ETC_choice

    clr_country_flag = has_preach_game
    clr_country_flag = has_argue_game
    parilament_choice_effect = yes

    refresh_bgt_seat = yes
}

        set_temp_variable = { eipc = -2 }
        set_temp_variable = { eiac = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { eamc = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { eaec = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { eaac = 2.5 }
        set_temp_variable = { eqc = 2.5 }
        set_temp_variable = { elc = -3 }
        set_temp_variable = { eic = 0 }
        cof_econ_target_change = yes 
    }

    #《经济救援法》
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = bill_economic_relief_act_vote }
        clr_country_flag = bill_economic_relief_act_vote

        add_ideas = bill_economic_relief_act1
        add_to_array = { array = FRA.cof_social_bills value = 16 }

        custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
        custom_effect_tooltip = effect_society
        set_temp_variable = { pop_wc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { pop_pc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { pop_mc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { pop_sc = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { pop_bc = -3 }
        set_temp_variable = { pop_ac = 0 }
        class_pop_change = yes
        
        custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
        set_temp_variable = { wc = 2 }
        set_temp_variable = { pc = 2 }
        set_temp_variable = { mc = 2 }
        set_temp_variable = { sc = 2 }
        set_temp_variable = { bc = -6 }
        set_temp_variable = { ac = 0 }
        class_pop_satisfactions_change = yes

        custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
        custom_effect_tooltip = effect_economy
        set_temp_variable = { ecc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { emc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { epc = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { eoc = 0 }
        Cof_economy_model_change = yes

        custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
        set_temp_variable = { evc = 2.5 }
        set_temp_variable = { eibc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { eipc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { eiac = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { eamc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { eaec = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { eaac = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { eqc = 3 }
        set_temp_variable = { elc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { eic = 0 }
        cof_econ_target_change = yes  
    }

    #《《全民基本福利法》
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = bill_universal_basic_benefits_vote }
        clr_country_flag = bill_universal_basic_benefits_vote

        add_ideas = bill_universal_basic_benefits1
        add_to_array = { array = FRA.cof_social_bills value = 17 }

        custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
        custom_effect_tooltip = effect_society
        set_temp_variable = { pop_wc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { pop_pc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { pop_mc = 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { pop_sc = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { pop_bc = -3 }
        set_temp_variable = { pop_ac = 0 }
        class_pop_change = yes
       
        custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
        set_temp_variable = { wc = 5 }
        set_temp_variable = { pc = 5 }
        set_temp_variable = { mc = 5 }
        set_temp_variable = { sc = 5 }
        set_temp_variable = { bc = -10 }
        set_temp_variable = { ac = 2.5 }
        class_pop_satisfactions_change = yes

        custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
        custom_effect_tooltip = effect_economy
        set_temp_variable = { evc = -5 }
        set_temp_variable = { eibc = -3 }
        set_temp_variable = { eipc = -2.5 }
        set_temp_variable = { eiac = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { eamc = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { eaec = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { eaac = 3 }
        set_temp_variable = { eqc = 6 }
        set_temp_variable = { elc = 0 }
        set_temp_variable = { eic = 0 }
        cof_econ_target_change = yes    
    }
}
