#       CSP态度变化
#       set_temp_variable = { target_a = 0 } # 1-DFA 2-DEA 3-DIS 4-DSRG 5-CGSC
#       set_temp_variable = { change_num = 0 } #+-1-3
#       CSP_attitude_change = yes
CSP_attitude_change = {
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { target_a = 1 } }
        add_to_variable = { DFA_attitude = change_num }
        clamp_variable = { var = DFA_attitude max = 5 min = -5 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { target_a = 2 } }
        add_to_variable = { DEA_attitude = change_num }
        clamp_variable = { var = DEA_attitude max = 5 min = -5 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { target_a = 3 } }
        add_to_variable = { DIS_attitude = change_num }
        clamp_variable = { var = DIS_attitude max = 5 min = -5 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { target_a = 4 } }
        add_to_variable = { DSRG_attitude = change_num }
        clamp_variable = { var = DSRG_attitude max = 5 min = -5 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { target_a = 5 } }
        add_to_variable = { CGSC_attitude = change_num }
        clamp_variable = { var = CGSC_attitude max = 5 min = -5 }
    }

    hidden_effect = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DFA_attitude = 5 } 
                    check_variable = { DFA_attitude = 4 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DFA_support
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DFA_attitude = 3 } 
                    check_variable = { DFA_attitude = 2 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DFA_cooperate
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DFA_attitude = 1 } 
                    check_variable = { DFA_attitude = 0 } 
                    check_variable = { DFA_attitude = -1 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DFA_neutrality
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DFA_attitude = -3 } 
                    check_variable = { DFA_attitude = -2 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DFA_dissatisfaction
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DFA_attitude = -4 } 
                    check_variable = { DFA_attitude = -5 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DFA_oppose
        }

        if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DEA_attitude = 5 } 
                    check_variable = { DEA_attitude = 4 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DEA_support
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DEA_attitude = 3 } 
                    check_variable = { DEA_attitude = 2 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DEA_cooperate
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DEA_attitude = 1 } 
                    check_variable = { DEA_attitude = 0 } 
                    check_variable = { DEA_attitude = -1 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DEA_neutrality
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DEA_attitude = -3 } 
                    check_variable = { DEA_attitude = -2 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DEA_dissatisfaction
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DEA_attitude = -4 } 
                    check_variable = { DEA_attitude = -5 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DEA_oppose
        }

        if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 5 } 
                    check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 4 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DIS_support
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 3 } 
                    check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 2 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DIS_cooperate
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 1 } 
                    check_variable = { DIS_attitude = 0 } 
                    check_variable = { DIS_attitude = -1 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DIS_neutrality
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DIS_attitude = -3 } 
                    check_variable = { DIS_attitude = -2 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DIS_dissatisfaction
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DIS_attitude = -4 } 
                    check_variable = { DIS_attitude = -5 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DIS_oppose
        }

        if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DSRG_attitude = 5 } 
                    check_variable = { DSRG_attitude = 4 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DSRG_support
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DSRG_attitude = 3 } 
                    check_variable = { DSRG_attitude = 2 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DSRG_cooperate
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DSRG_attitude = 1 } 
                    check_variable = { DSRG_attitude = 0 } 
                    check_variable = { DSRG_attitude = -1 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DSRG_neutrality
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DSRG_attitude = -3 } 
                    check_variable = { DSRG_attitude = -2 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DSRG_dissatisfaction
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { DSRG_attitude = -4 } 
                    check_variable = { DSRG_attitude = -5 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = DSRG_oppose
        }

        if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { CGSC_attitude = 5 } 
                    check_variable = { CGSC_attitude = 4 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = CGSC_support
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { CGSC_attitude = 3 } 
                    check_variable = { CGSC_attitude = 2 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = CGSC_cooperate
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { CGSC_attitude = 1 } 
                    check_variable = { CGSC_attitude = 0 } 
                    check_variable = { CGSC_attitude = -1 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = CGSC_neutrality
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { CGSC_attitude = -3 } 
                    check_variable = { CGSC_attitude = -2 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = CGSC_dissatisfaction
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    check_variable = { CGSC_attitude = -4 } 
                    check_variable = { CGSC_attitude = -5 } 
                }
            }
            add_ideas = CGSC_oppose
        }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { change_num > 0 } }
        custom_effect_tooltip = {
            localization_key = CSP_attitude_change_tt
            CHANGE_V = attitude_improvement
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { change_num < 0 } }
        custom_effect_tooltip = {
            localization_key = CSP_attitude_change_tt
            CHANGE_V = attitude_reduction
        }
    }
    else = {
        custom_effect_tooltip = CSP_attitude_change_no_tt
    }
}

###     根据情况改变态度
#       set_temp_variable = { synd_judge = 1 } -1-no 0-normal 1-yes
#       set_temp_variable = { oppo_judge = 1 }
#       set_temp_variable = { jaco_judge = 1 }
#       set_temp_variable = { sore_judge = 1 }
#       set_temp_variable = { target_a = 0 } # 1-DFA 2-DEA 3-DIS 4-DSRG 5-CGSC
#       set_temp_variable = { change_num = 0 } #+-1-3
#       CSP_attitude_faction_judge = yes
CSP_attitude_faction_judge = {
    #is this effect do improve attitude? -1 - no 0 - normal 1 - yes
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { target_a = 1 } }
        if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DFA_synd }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = synd_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DFA_oppo }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = oppo_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DFA_jaco }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = jaco_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DFA_sore }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = sore_judge }
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { target_a = 2 } }
        if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_synd }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = synd_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_oppo }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = oppo_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_jaco }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = jaco_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DEA_sore }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = sore_judge }
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { target_a = 3 } }
        if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DIS_synd }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = synd_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DIS_oppo }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = oppo_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DIS_jaco }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = jaco_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DIS_sore }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = sore_judge }
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { target_a = 4 } }
        if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DSRG_synd }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = synd_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DSRG_oppo }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = oppo_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DSRG_jaco }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = jaco_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = DSRG_sore }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = sore_judge }
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { target_a = 5 } }
        if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_synd }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = synd_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_oppo }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = oppo_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_jaco }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = jaco_judge }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = CGSC_sore }
            multiply_temp_variable = { change_num = sore_judge }
        }
    }

    CSP_attitude_change = yes
}

#妥协
party_choice_effect = {
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = party_cost_pp }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 1 } }
            add_political_power = -25
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 2 } }
            add_political_power = -50
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 3 } }
            add_political_power = -100
        }
    }

    else_if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = party_cost_economy }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 1 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = effect_economy
			set_temp_variable = { evc = -1 }
			set_temp_variable = { eibc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eipc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eiac = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eamc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eaec = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eaac = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eqc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { elc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eic = 0 }
			cof_econ_target_change = yes
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 2 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = effect_economy
			set_temp_variable = { evc = -2.5 }
			set_temp_variable = { eibc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eipc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eiac = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eamc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eaec = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eaac = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eqc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { elc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eic = 0 }
			cof_econ_target_change = yes
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 3 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = effect_economy
			set_temp_variable = { evc = -5 }
			set_temp_variable = { eibc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eipc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eiac = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eamc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eaec = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eaac = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eqc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { elc = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { eic = 0 }
			cof_econ_target_change = yes
        }
    }

    else_if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = party_cost_satisfation }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 1 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = effect_society
            set_temp_variable = { rnum = 1 }
            set_temp_variable = { rchange = -1 }
            random_pop_satisfation_change = yes      
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 2 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = effect_society
            set_temp_variable = { rnum = 2 }
            set_temp_variable = { rchange = -1.5 }
            random_pop_satisfation_change = yes      
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 3 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = effect_society
            set_temp_variable = { rnum = 3 }
            set_temp_variable = { rchange = -2 }
            random_pop_satisfation_change = yes      
        }
    }

    set_temp_variable = { vta_smc = 0 }
    set_temp_variable = { vta_src = 0 }
    set_temp_variable = { vta_occ = 0 }
    set_temp_variable = { vta_oac = 0 }
    set_temp_variable = { vta_jnc = 0 }
    set_temp_variable = { vta_jrc = 0 }
    set_temp_variable = { vta_soc = 0 }
    set_temp_variable = { vta_syc = 0 }
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 1 } }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tc = 2 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 2 } }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tc = 5 }
    } 
    else_if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { party_cost = 3 } }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tc = 10 }
    } 

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = party_choice_oppose }
        multiply_temp_variable = { vta_tc = -1 }
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = party_CNS_show }
        set_country_flag = party_CNS_choice
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { CNS_faction^1 > 0 } }
            set_temp_variable = { vta_smc = vta_tc }
        }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { CNS_faction^2 > 0 } }
            set_temp_variable = { vta_src = vta_tc }
        }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { CNS_faction^3 > 0 } }
            set_temp_variable = { vta_occ = vta_tc }
        }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { CNS_faction^4 > 0 } }

parilament_choice_effect = {
    clear_array = parilament_choice
    set_variable = { parilament_choice^1 = 14 }
    set_variable = { parilament_choice^2 = 14 }
    set_variable = { parilament_choice^3 = 14 }

    if = {
        limit = { 
            has_country_flag = voting_for_bill
            has_country_flag = has_preach_game
            has_country_flag = parilament_choice_preach
        }

        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^1 = 1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^1 = 13 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^1 = 0 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^1 = 14 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^1 = -1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^1 = 3 }
        }

        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^2 = 1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^2 = 13 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^2 = 0 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^2 = 14 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^2 = -1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^2 = 3 }
        }

        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^3 = 1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^3 = 13 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^3 = 0 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^3 = 14 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^3 = -1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^3 = 3 }
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            has_country_flag = voting_for_bill
            has_country_flag = has_argue_game
             has_country_flag = parilament_choice_argue
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^1 = 13 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 0 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^1 = 14 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = -1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^1 = 3 }
        }

        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^2 = 13 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 0 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^2 = 14 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = -1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^2 = 3 }
        }

        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^3 = 1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^3 = 13 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^3 = 0 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^3 = 14 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^3 = -1 } }
            set_variable = { parilament_choice^3 = 3 }
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = voting_for_bill } }
        set_variable = { parilament_choice^1 = 14 }
        set_variable = { parilament_choice^2 = 14 }
        set_variable = { parilament_choice^3 = 14 }
    }
}

parilament_choice_logic_rock = {
    add_political_power = -10
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = preach_gaming }
        hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 1 } }
				set_variable = { preach_game_p^1 = 1 }
				random_list = {
					1 = { set_variable = { preach_game_ai^1 = 1 } }
					1 = { set_variable = { preach_game_ai^1 = 2 } }
					1 = { set_variable = { preach_game_ai^1 = 3 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 2 } }
				set_variable = { preach_game_p^2 = 1 }
				random_list = {
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { preach_game^1 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { preach_game_ai^2 = 1 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { preach_game^1 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { preach_game_ai^2 = 2 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { preach_game^1 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { preach_game_ai^2 = 3 } 
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 3 } }
				set_variable = { preach_game_p^3 = 1 }
				random_list = {
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { preach_game^2 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { preach_game_ai^3 = 1 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { preach_game^2 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { preach_game_ai^3 = 2 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { preach_game^2 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { preach_game_ai^3 = 3 } 
					}
				}
			}
	
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = preach_game_ai^game_turn } }
				set_variable = { preach_game^game_turn = 0 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 1 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 2 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 2 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 3 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 3 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { preach_game^game_turn = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 1 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 3 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 2 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 1 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 3 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 2 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { preach_game^game_turn = -1 }
			}
	
			parilament_choice_effect = yes

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { game_turn > 2 }
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game^1 = 1 }
							check_variable = { preach_game^2 = 1 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game^1 = -1 }
							check_variable = { preach_game^2 = -1 }
						}
					}
				}
                country_event = cofpolitics.1005
			}
			else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 1 } }
                add_to_variable = { game_turn = 1 }
                country_event = cofpolitics.1003 
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 2 } }
                add_to_variable = { game_turn = 1 }
                country_event = cofpolitics.1004
            }
		}
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = argue_gaming }
        hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 1 } }
				set_variable = { argue_game_p^1 = 1 }
				random_list = {
					1 = { set_variable = { argue_game_ai^1 = 1 } }
					1 = { set_variable = { argue_game_ai^1 = 2 } }
					1 = { set_variable = { argue_game_ai^1 = 3 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 2 } }
				set_variable = { argue_game_p^2 = 1 }
				random_list = {
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^2 = 1 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^2 = 2 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^2 = 3 } 
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 3 } }
				set_variable = { argue_game_p^3 = 1 }
				random_list = {
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^3 = 1 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^3 = 2 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^3 = 3 } 
					}
				}
			}
	
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = argue_game_ai^game_turn } }
				set_variable = { argue_game^game_turn = 0 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 1 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 2 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 2 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 3 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 3 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { argue_game^game_turn = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 1 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 3 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 2 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 1 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 3 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 2 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { argue_game^game_turn = -1 }
			}
	
			parilament_choice_effect = yes

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { game_turn > 2 }
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 1 }
							check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 1 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game^1 = -1 }
							check_variable = { argue_game^2 = -1 }
						}
					}
				}
                
                country_event = cofpolitics.1005
			}
			else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 1 } }
                add_to_variable = { game_turn = 1 }
                country_event = cofpolitics.1003 
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 2 } }
                add_to_variable = { game_turn = 1 }
                country_event = cofpolitics.1004
            }
		}
    }
}

							NOT = { check_variable = { preach_game^2 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { preach_game_ai^3 = 3 } 
					}
				}
			}
	
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = preach_game_ai^game_turn } }
				set_variable = { preach_game^game_turn = 0 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 1 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 2 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 2 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 3 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 3 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { preach_game^game_turn = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 1 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 3 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 2 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 1 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game_p^game_turn = 3 }
							check_variable = { preach_game_ai^game_turn = 2 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { preach_game^game_turn = -1 }
			}
	
			parilament_choice_effect = yes

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { game_turn > 2 }
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game^1 = 1 }
							check_variable = { preach_game^2 = 1 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { preach_game^1 = -1 }
							check_variable = { preach_game^2 = -1 }
						}
					}
				}
                country_event = cofpolitics.1005
			}
			else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 1 } }
                add_to_variable = { game_turn = 1 }
                country_event = cofpolitics.1003 
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 2 } }
                add_to_variable = { game_turn = 1 }
                country_event = cofpolitics.1004
            }
		}
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = argue_gaming }
        hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 1 } }
				set_variable = { argue_game_p^1 = 3 }
				random_list = {
					1 = { set_variable = { argue_game_ai^1 = 1 } }
					1 = { set_variable = { argue_game_ai^1 = 2 } }
					1 = { set_variable = { argue_game_ai^1 = 3 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 2 } }
				set_variable = { argue_game_p^2 = 3 }
				random_list = {
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^2 = 1 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^2 = 2 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^2 = 3 } 
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 3 } }
				set_variable = { argue_game_p^3 = 3 }
				random_list = {
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^3 = 1 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^3 = 2 } 
					}
					1 = { 
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 0 } }
						}
						set_variable = { argue_game_ai^3 = 3 } 
					}
				}
			}
	
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = argue_game_ai^game_turn } }
				set_variable = { argue_game^game_turn = 0 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 1 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 2 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 2 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 3 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 3 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { argue_game^game_turn = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 1 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 3 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 2 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 1 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game_p^game_turn = 3 }
							check_variable = { argue_game_ai^game_turn = 2 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { argue_game^game_turn = -1 }
			}
	
			parilament_choice_effect = yes
			

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { game_turn > 2 }
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 1 }
							check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 1 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { argue_game^1 = -1 }
							check_variable = { argue_game^2 = -1 }
						}
					}
				}
                country_event = cofpolitics.1005
			}
			else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 1 } }
                add_to_variable = { game_turn = 1 }
                country_event = cofpolitics.1003 
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { game_turn = 2 } }
                add_to_variable = { game_turn = 1 }
                country_event = cofpolitics.1004
            }
		}
    }
}

parliament_result_judge = {
    set_temp_variable = { game_win = 0 }
    set_temp_variable = { game_draw = 0 }
    set_temp_variable = { game_lose = 0 }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = preach_gaming }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^1 = 1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_win = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^1 = 0 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_draw = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^1 = -1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_lose = 1 }
        }
    
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^2 = 1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_win = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^2 = 0 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_draw = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^2 = -1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_lose = 1 }
        }
    
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^3 = 1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_win = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^3 = 0 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_draw = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { preach_game^3 = -1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_lose = 1 }
        }
    }
    
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = argue_gaming }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_win = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = 0 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_draw = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^1 = -1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_lose = 1 }
        }
    
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_win = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = 0 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_draw = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^2 = -1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_lose = 1 }
        }
    
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^3 = 1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_win = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^3 = 0 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_draw = 1 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { argue_game^3 = -1 } }
            add_to_temp_variable = { game_lose = 1 }
        }
    }

    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { game_win = 2 }
            check_variable = { game_draw = 0 }
            check_variable = { game_lose = 0 }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tct = 8 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { game_win = 2 }
            check_variable = { game_draw = 1 }
            check_variable = { game_lose = 0 }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tct = 6 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { game_win = 2 }
            check_variable = { game_draw = 0 }
            check_variable = { game_lose = 1 }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tct = 4 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { game_win = 1 }
            check_variable = { game_draw = 2 }
            check_variable = { game_lose = 0 }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tct = 2 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                AND = {
                    check_variable = { game_win = 0 }
                    check_variable = { game_draw = 3 }
                    check_variable = { game_lose = 0 }
                }
                AND = {
                    check_variable = { game_win = 1 }
                    check_variable = { game_draw = 1 }
                    check_variable = { game_lose = 1 }
                }
            }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tct = 0 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { game_win = 0 }
            check_variable = { game_draw = 2 }
            check_variable = { game_lose = 1 }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tct = -1 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { game_win = 1 }
            check_variable = { game_draw = 0 }
            check_variable = { game_lose = 2 }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tct = -2 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { game_win = 0 }
            check_variable = { game_draw = 1 }
            check_variable = { game_lose = 2 }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tct = -3 }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { game_win = 0 }
            check_variable = { game_draw = 0 }
            check_variable = { game_lose = 2 }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_tct = -4 }
    }

    if = { limit = { has_country_flag = game_support }}
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = game_anti }
        multiply_temp_variable = { vta_tct = -1 }
    }
    
    if = { limit = { check_variable = { vta_tct = 0 } } }
    else = {
        custom_effect_tooltip = effect_politics
        set_temp_variable = { vta_smc = vta_tct }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_src = vta_tct }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_occ = vta_tct }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_oac = vta_tct }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_jnc = vta_tct }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_jrc = vta_tct }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_soc = vta_tct }
        set_temp_variable = { vta_syc = vta_tct }
        Cof_politics_faction_agree_vote_change = yes
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = preach_gaming }
        clr_country_flag = preach_gaming
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = argue_gaming }
        clr_country_flag = argue_gaming
    }

    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = game_support }
        clr_country_flag = game_support
    }
    if = {
        limit = { has_country_flag = game_anti }
        clr_country_flag = game_anti
    }
}

Cof_booming_youth_culture_movement_update = {
    if = {
        limit = { NOT = { has_idea = Cof_booming_youth_culture_movement1 } }
        effect_tooltip = { add_ideas = Cof_booming_youth_culture_movement1 }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { seat_sore_yout > 80 } }
            hidden_effect = { add_ideas = Cof_booming_youth_culture_movement1 }
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_idea = Cof_booming_youth_culture_movement1 }
        effect_tooltip = { 
            swap_ideas = {
                remove_idea = Cof_booming_youth_culture_movement1
                add_idea = Cof_booming_youth_culture_movement2
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { seat_sore_yout > 80 }  }
            hidden_effect = { 
                swap_ideas = {
                    remove_idea = Cof_booming_youth_culture_movement1
                    add_idea = Cof_booming_youth_culture_movement2
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts_update = {
    if = {
        limit = { has_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts1 }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts1
            add_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts2
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts2 }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts2
            add_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts3
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts3 }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts3
            add_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts4
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts4 }
        swap_ideas = {
            remove_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts4
            add_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts5
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_idea = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts5 }
        remove_ideas = Cof_intensified_urban_rural_conflicts5
    }
}
